<?xml version="1.0"?>

  <!-- owl:Class declarations -->

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Player">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An individual who participates in a game or activity.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A structured activity or contest with rules, often played for enjoyment.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Achievement">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A milestone, award, or accomplishment earned by a player in a game or activity.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GamePlaySession">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An instance of a player engaging with a game for a specific period of time.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Play Session</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AchievementType">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement Type</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Genre">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Genre</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Item">

</owl:Class>

</owl:Class>

</owl:Class>

</owl:Class>

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Statistic Type</rdfs:label>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PlayerItemPossession">

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Equipment">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game">

  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Ability</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PlayerGameStatistic">

  <!-- owl:Class declarations -->

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Player">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An individual who participates in a game or activity.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Game">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A structured activity or contest with rules, often played for enjoyment.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Achievement">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A milestone, award, or accomplishment earned by a player in a game or activity.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#GamePlaySession">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An instance of a player engaging with a game for a specific period of time.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Game Play Session</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#AchievementType">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A category or classification of achievements, such as 'combat', 'exploration', or 'crafting'.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Achievement Type</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Genre">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A category or style of a game, such as Action, Role-Playing, Strategy, or Simulation.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Genre</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Item">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A collectible, usable, or interactive object within a game world, such as a weapon, potion, or key.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Item</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Ability">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A power, skill, or effect that an item can grant or perform, such as dealing damage, healing, or unlocking a door.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Ability</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PlayerGameStatistic">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A record of a specific statistic (e.g., kill count, score, play time) for a player in a particular game.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player Game Statistic</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#StatisticType">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A category or name of a measurable statistic in a game, such as 'KillCount', 'Score', or 'TimePlayed'.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Statistic Type</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PlayerItemPossession">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A record representing a player's possession of a specific item, which can include details like quantity or acquisition time.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player Item Possession</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PlayerGameCompletion">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A record representing a player's completion status for a specific game, particularly regarding achievements.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Player Game Completion</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Equipment">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A type of item that a player can use or wear to enhance their capabilities in a game, such as weapons, armor, or tools.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Equipment</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:subClassOf rdf:resource='http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Item'/>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#ItemUsageEvent">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">An event representing a player using a specific item within a game, potentially during a play session.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Item Usage Event</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#InAppPurchase">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A record of a player making a purchase within a game application, such as buying virtual currency, items, or content.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">In-App Purchase</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PlayerGameFirstPurchaseTime">

</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#PlayingArea">
